[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  An AddressSanitizer crash shows an “attempting double-free” on a [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m-byte memory [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion. The region is allocated via xmlFuzzMalloc/xmlStrndup and freed twice inside[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlParseAttribute2 in parser.c. This triggers an immediate abort when the second [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfree is performed.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Double-free of heap memory. This can lead to memory corruption, undefined [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior, and possible security exploitation if an attacker can control subsequent [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap allocations.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    ret[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In xmlParseAttribute2 [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the local pointer `internal_val` is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated via `xmlStrndup`.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For the special attribute `xml:tab`, when the value is invalid [0m[1;39m([0m[39melse branch at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m9018[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code calls `[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` immediately [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m9024[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthen—unconditionally—calls `[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` again at line [0m[1;36m9028[0m[39m. This [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free triggers the AddressSanitizer abort.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar attribute‐handling branches [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `xml:space`, `xml:lang`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m do not [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreemptively free `internal_val`, instead relying solely on the final `xmlFree` at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe end of the function. [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Remove the redundant free in the invalid-value branch for `xml:tab`:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In parser.c, locate xmlParseAttribute2 around lines [0m[1;36m9008[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m9028[0m[39m.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In the `else` block for unrecognized tab values, delete the line:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After removal, the warning message will still be emitted, and the unified [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfree at line [0m[1;36m9028[0m[39m will correctly release the allocation exactly once.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Alternative guard [0m[1;39m([0m[39mless preferred[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: If retaining the early free is desired, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately nullify `internal_val` after freeing it:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         internal_val = NULL;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Then the final `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` is skipped. [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, simply removing the early free aligns this branch with the other attribute[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcases and avoids confusion.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We keep the warning message for invalid `xml:tab` values untouched.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We preserve the single, unified deallocation at the end of xmlParseAttribute2,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring no memory leaks in normal or error paths.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other branches [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`default`, `preserve`, `expand`, `skip`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are unaffected and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to set `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt->tab[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` appropriately.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. No Side Effects on Fuzzing or Tests[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This patch only modifies parser.c; fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxml.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and tests remain [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntouched.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer will trigger the same code paths but will no longer abort on [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free; instead, invalid `xml:tab` values will generate warnings and then free[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monce.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new exceptions are caught or broad error-handling logic added, so we [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintain the strict contract of `xmlStrndup`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`xmlFree`.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Open parser.c.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Navigate to xmlParseAttribute2 [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m9008[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlStrEqual[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, BAD_CAST [0m[32m"tab"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block, remove the [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` statement inside the invalid-value `else`.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild and re-run the libFuzzer XML harness to confirm the double-free no [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger occurs and no leak is introduced.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run full test suite to ensure no regressions.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removing the redundant free exactly addresses the double-free without altering[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation or final cleanup logic.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It aligns handling of `xml:tab` with other attributes in this function, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintaining consistency and simplicity.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This minimal change yields the maximum clarity and maintains all intended [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwarnings, correct defaulting, and a single free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:    ret = [0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m len + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mret == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret, cur, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    ret[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In xmlParseAttribute2 [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the `xml:tab`‐processing branch allocates a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtemporary string [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`internal_val`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with [0m[1;35mxmlStrndup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On encountering an invalid value, it calls `[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` inside the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`else` warning block, then falls through to an unconditional `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` immediately afterward—resulting in a double‐free.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The last patch attempt removed the first free call but accidentally shifted [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbraces and labels, breaking control flow and causing compilation errors.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The surrounding error‐handling labels [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mem_error`, `error`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the final [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanup of `val` under those labels must remain untouched.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The xml:space branch and the normal return path should continue to function [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly as before.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness or test code changes are required.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Minimal, Safe Patch Strategy  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In the malformed‐value branch for `xml:tab`, restore the free of [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`internal_val` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mso the warning block continues to release the buffer it just [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Immediately after freeing `internal_val` in that branch, set `internal_val = [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNULL;`.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the subsequent `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` intact. Since[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`internal_val` is now NULL after the first free, the second free will be skipped.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Do not touch any surrounding braces, labels, or other logic.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Implementation Steps  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Open parser.c and navigate to the xml:tab handling around line [0m[1;36m9020[0m[39m.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Modify the invalid‐value `else` block as follows [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly the three lines inside [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat block change[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```diff[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mxmlWarningMsg[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, XML_WAR_TAB_VALUE,[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                        [0m[32m"Invalid value \"%s\" for xml:tab : \"default\", [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m\"preserve\", \"expand\", or \"skip\" expected\n"[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                        internal_val, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-         [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+         [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+         internal_val = NULL;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other deletions, insertions, or brace‐movements are required.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By nulling `internal_val` after the first free, the later `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal_val[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest fails, so the second free is eliminated.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch is minimal and localized, preserving all original control‐flow [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstructures, error labels, and cleanup code.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It directly targets the identified double‐free without impacting xml:space [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing or other parts of xmlParseAttribute2.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification & Side‐Effect Analysis  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that xml:tab invalid values still emit a warning and free their [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtemporary buffer.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure that memory is still freed exactly once in all code paths.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Build and run existing unit tests and the fuzz harness—there should be no new [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompiler errors, and the double‐free must be resolved.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Since `internal_val` is a local pointer and not used beyond this block except [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor the common cleanup, setting it to NULL has no unintended side effects.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
